There is also a large lawn and some small amusement facilities inside the hotel, but I didn't experience them because I was in a hurry... There are basically no nearby restaurants, and the nearest ones are all in Maoshan Scenic Area. The hotel buffet costs 158 per person, and it is more than 17 kilometers away from Jurong City... Overall, I am satisfied. If the price can be not so high during holidays, I will be more satisfied.

info:Superior Street View King Room
info:Stayed in December 2023
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted December 26, 2023
msg:As expected of being owned by the Intercontinental Group, the hardware and software levels of this Holiday Inn are pretty good. The hotel thoughtfully upgraded the lake view room for free. The room is larger and cleaner. There is a private hot spring pool on the balcony. The nameplate on it states the ingredients of natural mineral water. You can soak in the hot spring as many times as you like. It takes about 20 minutes to fill the pool with water. There are curtains on the balcony, which can be drawn up for more privacy when bathing. The air conditioning is very powerful, the heating is very hot, and the toilet has a Washlet smart toilet seat. The buffet breakfast has many varieties, including local specialty pot noodles and pancakes. The area near the hotel is relatively desolate and is suitable for self-driving tours. Taking a taxi is probably difficult. Maoshan Town, which is a three- to five-minute drive from the hotel, does not have much food except some farm dishes.
The hotel's underground parking lot is the only place that doesn't feel good. It's a bit dirty and has insufficient lighting. It's not in line with the positioning of a hotel of this level. It may be shared with Piandao Hot Spring.
